are dedicated to provide a holistic STEM-based and tech-enabled curriculum 
to ensure our children are P1-ready and equipped with future-ready 
mindsets.">

      <div class="sqs-layout sqs-grid-12 columns-12" data-type="page-section" id="page-section-6494a115d15eb00debf9dd79"><div class="row sqs-row" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711868202139_186"><div class="col sqs-col-12 span-12" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711868202139_185"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-d1800b8da2ab7af6301b"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.109924s;"><strong>Ang Mo Kio Methodist Preschool provides 3-hour Playgroup (PG) programme for children aged 18 months to 2 years old as well as 4-hour and 6-hour preschool programmes for children 2 to 6 years old at the Pre-Nursery to K2 levels. We are located within the spacious compound of Ang Mo Kio Methodist Church and have been serving families in the Ang Mo Kio, Yio Chu Kang and neighbouring estates since 1982. </strong></p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.114504s;"><strong>Children enjoy and benefit from experiential learning of concept-based tasks through a balance of exploration and play-based activities. Our holistic STEM-based, tech-enabled curriculum coupled with thematic-based learning prepare our children for P1 and beyond. </strong></p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.119084s;"><strong>Our team of qualified and experienced educators are well-trained to ensure that children cultivate healthy habits, positive learning dispositions and good values through Christian education. We are committed to  nurture every child to be a person of Good Character, with future-ready mindsets of an Explorer, an Innovator and an Entrepreneur. </strong></p>
</div>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.146565s;"><span class="sqsrte-text-color--custom" style="color: #E31919"><strong>Ang Mo Kio Methodist Preschool has received the 2024 Three Best Rated Preschools Award in Ang Mo Kio.</strong></span></p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div><div class="sqs-block markdown-block sqs-block-markdown" data-block-type="44" id="block-e6586bfa3b022b5fa066"><div class="sqs-block-content"><p class="preFade" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.151145s;"><span data-preserve-html-node="true" class="readMore">Read More</span></p>
<p class="show preFade" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.155725s;">Three Best Rated (Singapore) was created in 2014 with a goal to identify the top 3 local businesses  in a locale based on the quality of the business. The businesses are picked using Three Best Rated 50-Point Inspection, an extensive analysis of the business' reputation, history, complaints, ratings, satisfaction, trust, cost, general excellence, etc. The process is done by trained business analysts of Three Best Rated. Businesses do not pay Three Best to be listed.</p>
<p class="show preFade" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.160305s;">Ang Mo Kio Methodist Preschool has received the 2024 Three Best Rated Award for Preschools in Ang Mo Kio and listed as one of the Top 3 Preschools in Ang Mo Kio.</p>

    </div>

  <h2 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.174046s;" class="preSlide"><em>Principals Message</em></h2><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.178626s;"><strong>MRS PRISCILLA LOW</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.183206s;">Hello, I am Priscilla, principal of Ang Mo Kio Methodist Preschool.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.187786s;">I am happy that our school is now a part of the family of Methodist preschools. It is a privilege for me to serve here with a team of dedicated teachers who derive joy in nurturing young children.  The teachers here are professionally trained to support the childrens learning and development in their preschool years.  Everyone works together as a big family and always looking out for each other.  We value the partnership with families as well and work closely with parents to help children develop to their best potential.</p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.192366s;">We adopt an experiential approach in teaching and learning to enable children to have fun in a safe environment. The joy that each child experiences in learning is priceless.  Apart from fun and active learning, emphasis is given to nurture young childrens social-emotional development and character to shape them for life.  We believe that with positive affirmation and opportunities, every child has the potential to excel.  </p><p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.196947s;">Come visit us at Ang Mo Kio Methodist Preschool today.</p>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.29771s;"><strong>The Explorers programme is one of the programmes offered in our curriculum. Co-designed by The Boys Brigade Singapore and Girls Brigade Singapore, it is a programme with a rich heritage of time-tested expertise, passion and experience that have shown effective results of developing great character values and instilling important life skills in children.&nbsp; Each lesson contains a story pertaining to a life lesson attached to a value and with purposeful activities to engage in. &nbsp; </strong></p>

</div></div></div></div></section><a class="c-tabs__accordion-tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="tabpanel--earth-day-" id="tab--earth-day-" href="#tabpanel--earth-day-" aria-expanded="false" style="display: none;"><span class="c-tabs__tab-title"><img data-preserve-html-node="true" src="https://static1.squarespace.com/static/5fe9e26f8d20536a3fc01415/t/610a490c7244840303583aaf/1628064012412/Group+67.png" alt="" title="" width="60" height="60"> Earth Day <br data-preserve-html-node="true"> </span></a><section class="c-tabs__tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab--earth-day-" id="tabpanel--earth-day-" style="display: none;"><div class="c-tabs__tabpanel-inner"><div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-3a29f4101032594d8787"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.30687s;"><strong>We celebrate Earth Day in our centre annually. Earth Day is celebrated worldwide on 22 April to honor the achievements of the environmental movement and to raise awareness of the need to protect Earths natural resources for future generations.  We invite parents to join us in our annual celebration as part of our efforts to inculcate the important value of environmental preservation and how everyone, including children can play a part in it in protecting Mother Earth.</strong></p>

Even when we moved further away from AMK, we chose to stick with this school and bear the inconvenience of long commutes every day.&amp;nbsp; <\/p><p class=\&quot;\&quot; style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap;\&quot;>Through the schools computer literacy programme, Michael has also nurtured a love for coding and robotics - kudos to the school for incorporating this into the curriculum and for nurturing teachers who really care about the children! <\/p><p class=\&quot;\&quot; style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap;\&quot;>Even though Michael graduates from K2 this year, it was an easy decision to enrol our second son Matthias in N1 next year.&amp;nbsp; <\/p><p class=\&quot;\&quot; style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap;\&quot;>Thank you AMK Methodist Preschool for the wonderful experience! <\/p><p class=\&quot;\&quot; style=\&quot;white-space:pre-wrap;\&quot;><em>-Parents of Michael Ooi<\/em> <\/p>&quot;,

        const firstSection = document.querySelector('.page-section');

<!-- Add Section IDs for anchor links -->
<script>
(function () {
  window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    var sections = document.querySelectorAll('section');
    var windowPath = window.location.pathname;
    // If page is set to homepage then set the anchor to home. i.e. #home-1
    if (windowPath === '/') {
      windowPath = 'home';
    }

    var anchorID = windowPath.replace('/', '');

    sections.forEach((section, i) => {
      section.id = `${anchorID}-${i+1}`;
    })
  })
})()
</script>

<script>
window.onscroll = function() {myFunction()};

function myFunction() {
  var winScroll = document.body.scrollTop || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
  var height = document.documentElement.scrollHeight - document.documentElement.clientHeight;
  var scrolled = (winScroll / height) * 100;
  document.getElementById("progressBar").style.width = scrolled + "%";
}
